\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{axes3d_8py_source_l04110}04110\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ The\ quaternion\ for\ the\ shortest\ rotation\ from\ vector\ r1\ to\ vector\ r2}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{axes3d_8py_source_l04111}04111\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ i.e.,\ q\ =\ sqrt(r2*r1'),\ normalized.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{axes3d_8py_source_l04112}04112\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ If\ r1\ and\ r2\ are\ antiparallel,\ then\ the\ result\ is\ ambiguous;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{axes3d_8py_source_l04113}04113\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ a\ normal\ vector\ will\ be\ returned,\ and\ a\ warning\ will\ be\ issued.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{axes3d_8py_source_l04114}04114\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ "{}"{}"{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{axes3d_8py_source_l04115}04115\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ k\ =\ np.cross(r1,\ r2)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{axes3d_8py_source_l04116}04116\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ nk\ =\ np.linalg.norm(k)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{axes3d_8py_source_l04117}04117\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ th\ =\ np.arctan2(nk,\ np.dot(r1,\ r2))}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{axes3d_8py_source_l04118}04118\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ th\ /=\ 2}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{axes3d_8py_source_l04119}04119\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ if\ nk\ ==\ 0:\ \ \#\ r1\ and\ r2\ are\ parallel\ or\ anti-\/parallel}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{axes3d_8py_source_l04120}04120\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ if\ np.dot(r1,\ r2)\ <\ 0:}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{axes3d_8py_source_l04121}04121\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ warnings.warn("{}Rotation\ defined\ by\ anti-\/parallel\ vectors\ is\ ambiguous"{})}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{axes3d_8py_source_l04122}04122\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ k\ =\ np.zeros(3)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{axes3d_8py_source_l04123}04123\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ k[np.argmin(r1*r1)]\ =\ 1\ \ \#\ basis\ vector\ most\ perpendicular\ to\ r1-\/r2}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{axes3d_8py_source_l04124}04124\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ k\ =\ np.cross(r1,\ k)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{axes3d_8py_source_l04125}04125\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ k\ =\ k\ /\ np.linalg.norm(k)\ \ \#\ unit\ vector\ normal\ to\ r1-\/r2}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{axes3d_8py_source_l04126}04126\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ q\ =\ cls(0,\ k)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{axes3d_8py_source_l04127}04127\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ else:}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{axes3d_8py_source_l04128}04128\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ q\ =\ cls(1,\ [0,\ 0,\ 0])\ \ \#\ =\ 1,\ no\ rotation}
